                       You'll get the entire private, ground floor apartment, on a clean canal, minutes from Florida Bay.                       <div data-reactid="633">
                       The apartment is private, uber clean and cozy. There is a large yard with our boat dock, kayak ramp and a floating launch dock. The sunsets are cool as the sky is usually colorful at night. About the kayaks: We have two Hobie Mirage-Drive kayaks for your use. If you are unfamiliar with these kayaks, you can drive them hands-free since your legs are doing the propulsion forward. It's super easy to go very fast, or very far, with minimal effort. So you'll have your hands free to take pictures, hold a beer, go fishing, whatever. For more info; Go to YOUTUBE and search 'Hobie Mirage-Drive Kayaks'. We also have two (2) stand-up paddle boards. Nobody offers these amenities for free anymore, but we do! You may want to visit historic Key West, while you are here. The drive is very easy, and takes about 1.5 hours typically. The views are iconic and beautiful as you pass the old seven-mile bridge, the Key deer sanctuary, and miles of sparkling blue-green ocean surrounding you on both sides.

                       Tommy Bahama style studio apartment underneath our personal home. Located on a beautiful, deep water, swimming canal with direct ocean &amp; bay access. Bring your boat for world-class fishing, diving &amp; snorkeling! Great restaurants &amp; shopping nearby!

                      <div data-reactid="1017">
                       This is a studio apartment underneath our home. The house is on pilings, we live upstairs and rent the apartment, which is at ground level with it's own private entrance. The apartment is basically like a hotel room, beautifully decorated in Tommy Bahama furnishings. It has a new, queen size bed plus a daybed that turns into a king-size bed. The room can comfortably sleep 2 adults &amp; 2 children. There is not a kitchen inside the apartment, but there is a mini-refrigerator, microwave &amp; keurig coffee maker. There is a full-size refrigerator &amp; charcoal BBQ grill on the back porch for guest use. There is also a sink, fish cleaning station with hose and shower dockside which overlooks a clear swimming canal with direct ocean and easy bay access. Canal has tons of little tropical fish, lobster and occasionally a manatee or two! Property has tons of tropical foliage &amp; about 25 coconut palm trees. We are almost finished installing a beautiful free-form pool, spa and tiki hut. Will be complete in March 2017.

There are lots of mangrove trails to explore by water. The beautiful reefs of the Florida Keys are just 3 miles away! Snorkel, dive &amp; fishing charters are nearby.
